{"id":"ca92ff28-607b-4f65-aad6-a4666801e942","identifier":"FRG-244","title":"Characters face toward objects when interacting","description":"## Problem

When a character arrives at an object, they keep whatever facing direction they had from walking. Sol uses the kotatsu but faces left instead of toward it.

## Root Cause

\\_handleObjectArrival in Engine.js calls char.startInteraction() but never sets char.facing based on the object position.

## What to do

1. In \\_handleObjectArrival, calculate facing direction from character position to object tile
2. Set char.facing before calling startInteraction()
3. Same for \\_startConversation — characters should face each other

## Acceptance Criteria

* Character faces the object they are interacting with
* Characters face each other during conversations

    47→      get hour() { return Math.floor(this.minuteOfDay / 60); },
    48→      get minute() { return Math.floor(this.minuteOfDay % 60); },

   180→  // ── Event bus ──

   182→  on(eventType, callback) {

   184→      this.listeners.set(eventType, new Set());
   185→    }

   194→  _emit(eventType, data) {

   196→    if (callbacks) {

   198→        cb(data);
   199→      }

   202→    const wildcards = this.listeners.get('*');
   203→    if (wildcards) {
   204→      for (const cb of wildcards) {

   206→      }
   207→    }
   208→  }

   210→  // ── Character AI / Wander behavior ──

   212→  _wanderTick() {
   213→    // Advance simulated clock each tick
   214→    this.simClock.advance();
   215→
   216→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   217→      if (char.action !== 'idle') continue;
   218→
   219→      // AI mode: delegate to AI decision engine
   220→      if (this.aiMode && this.aiEngine) {
   221→        if (!this.aiEngine.isPending(char.id)) {
   222→          this.aiEngine.tick(char, this.tickIntervalMs);
   223→        }
   224→        continue;
   225→      }
   226→
   227→      // Random wander with cooldown
   228→      char.wanderCooldown -= this.tickIntervalMs;
   229→      if (char.wanderCooldown > 0) continue;
   230→
   231→      // Priority actions first (reactive behavior), then random wander
   232→      const priority = this._getPriorityTarget(char);
   233→      const target = priority ? priority.obj : this._pickWanderTarget(char);
   234→      const action = priority ? priority.action : 'use';
   235→
   236→      if (!target) {
   237→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   238→        continue;
   239→      }
   240→
   241→      const tile = findInteractTile(target.position);
   242→      if (!tile) {
   243→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   244→        continue;
   245→      }
   246→
   247→      // Already adjacent — interact directly
   248→      const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);
   249→      if (atTarget) {
   250→        this._doInteraction(char, target, action);
   251→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;
   252→      } else if (char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   253→        char.targetObjectId = target.id;
   254→        char.pendingAction = action;
   255→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;
   256→      } else {
   257→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   258→      }
   259→    }
   260→  }
   261→
   262→  /** Immediate random wander (no cooldown) — used as AI fallback. */
   263→  _randomWander(char) {
   264→    const priority = this._getPriorityTarget(char);
   265→    const target = priority ? priority.obj : this._pickWanderTarget(char);
   266→    const action = priority ? priority.action : 'use';
   267→
   268→    if (!target) return;
   269→
   270→    const tile = findInteractTile(target.position);
   271→    if (!tile) return;
   272→
   273→    const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);
   274→    if (atTarget) {
   275→      this._doInteraction(char, target, action);
   276→    } else if (char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   277→      char.targetObjectId = target.id;
   278→      char.pendingAction = action;
   279→    }
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  _updateCharacters(deltaMs) {
   283→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   284→      const wasWalking = char.action === 'walking';
   285→      char.update(deltaMs);
   286→
   287→      // Character just arrived at destination
   288→      if (wasWalking && char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
   289→        const obj = this.objectEngine.get(char.targetObjectId);
   290→        if (obj) {
   291→          this._doInteraction(char, obj, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   292→        } else {
   293→          char.targetObjectId = null;
   294→        }
   295→        char.pendingAction = 'use';
   296→      }
   297→    }
   298→  }
   299→
   300→  _doInteraction(char, obj, action = 'use') {
   301→    // Face toward the object
   302→    const objCx = obj.position.tx + (obj.position.tw || 1) / 2;
   303→    const objCy = obj.position.ty + (obj.position.th || 1) / 2;
   304→    const dx = objCx - char.tx;
   305→    const dy = objCy - char.ty;
   306→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   307→      char._updateFacing(dx, 0);
   308→    } else {
   309→      char._updateFacing(0, dy);
   310→    }
   311→
   312→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(obj.id, action);
   313→    if (event) {
   314→      char.startInteraction(obj.id);
   315→
   316→      // Successful interaction → happy (unless already upset)
   317→      if (char.mood !== 'upset') {
   318→        char.setMood('happy', 5000);
   319→      }
   320→
   321→      this._emit('character:interact', {
   322→        characterId: char.id, characterName: char.name,
   323→        objectId: obj.id, objectName: event.objectName,
   324→        from: event.from, to: event.to,
   325→        produces: event.produces || null,
   326→        emoji: event.emoji || null,
   327→      });
   328→    } else {
   329→      char.targetObjectId = null;
   330→    }
   331→  }
   332→
   333→  _getPriorityTarget(char) {
   334→    // Sol: pick up book if closed and nearby
   335→    if (char.id === 'sol') {
   336→      const book = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_book');
   337→      if (book && book.state === 'closed') {
   338→        const dist = Math.abs(book.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(book.position.ty - char.ty);
   339→        if (dist <= 6) {
   340→          return { obj: book, action: 'use' };
   341→        }
   342→      }
   343→    }
   344→
   345→    // Non-Maple near stocked display → take pastry
   346→    if (char.id !== 'maple') {
   347→      const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   348→      if (display && display.state === 'stocked') {
   349→        const dist = Math.abs(display.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(display.position.ty - char.ty);
   350→        if (dist <= 8) {
   351→          return { obj: display, action: 'use' };
   352→        }
   353→      }
   354→    }
   355→
   356→    // Maple: restock empty display case
   357→    if (char.id === 'maple') {
   358→      const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   359→      if (display && display.state === 'empty') {
   360→        return { obj: display, action: 'use' };
   361→      }
   362→    }
   363→
   364→    return null;
   365→  }
   366→
   367→  _pickWanderTarget(char) {
   368→    const allObjects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   369→
   370→    // 60% home sector, 40% any sector
   371→    let candidates;
   372→    if (Math.random() < 0.6) {
   373→      candidates = allObjects.filter(o => o.sector === char.homeSector);
   374→      if (candidates.length === 0) candidates = allObjects;
   375→    } else {
   376→      candidates = allObjects;
   377→    }
   378→
   379→    // Avoid repeating last interaction
   380→    if (char.lastObjectId && candidates.length > 1) {
   381→      candidates = candidates.filter(o => o.id !== char.lastObjectId);
   382→    }
   383→
   384→    if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
   385→    return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
   386→  }
   387→
   388→  _reactToObjectEvent(event) {
   389→    // Espresso done → Maple happy
   390→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_espresso' && event.to === 'done') {
   391→      const maple = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'maple');
   392→      if (maple) maple.setMood('happy', 10000);
   393→    }
   394→
   395→    // Easel finished → Nyx happy
   396→    if (event.objectId === 'apt_easel' && event.to === 'finished') {
   397→      const nyx = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'nyx');
   398→      if (nyx) nyx.setMood('happy', 20000);
   399→    }
   400→
   401→    // Display restocked → nearby characters happy
   402→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_display' && event.to === 'stocked') {
   403→      for (const char of this.characters) {
   404→        const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   405→        if (display) {
   406→          const dist = Math.abs(display.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(display.position.ty - char.ty);
   407→          if (dist <= 6) char.setMood('happy', 10000);
   408→        }
   409→      }
   410→    }
   411→  }
   412→
   413→  // ── Internal loop ──
   414→
   415→  _loop() {
   416→    if (!this.running) return;
   417→
   418→    this._rafId = requestAnimationFrame((timestamp) => {
   419→      if (!this.running) return;
   420→
   421→      if (!this.paused) {
   422→        const rawDelta = timestamp - this._lastTimestamp;
   423→        const delta = Math.min(rawDelta, 500) * this.timeScale; // cap delta, apply scale
   424→
   425→        this._accumulator += delta;
   426→
   427→        // Process full ticks
   428→        while (this._accumulator >= this.tickIntervalMs) {
   429→          this._accumulator -= this.tickIntervalMs;
   430→          const tickEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(this.tickIntervalMs);
   431→          this.tickCount++;
   432→          this.elapsedMs += this.tickIntervalMs;
   433→
   434→          this._wanderTick();
   435→
   436→          this._emit('engine:tick', {
   437→            tickCount: this.tickCount,
   438→            elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs,
   439→            events: tickEvents,
   440→          });
   441→        }
   442→
   443→        // Smooth character movement each frame
   444→        this._updateCharacters(delta);
   445→      }
   446→
   447→      this._lastTimestamp = timestamp;
   448→      this._loop();
   449→    });
   450→  }
   451→}

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #23
The code already has the facing logic in `_doInteraction`. Looking at lines 300-310: ```javascript _doInteraction(char, obj, action = 'use') { // Face toward the object const objCx = obj.position.tx + (obj.position.tw || 1) / 2; const objCy = obj.position.ty + (obj.position.th || 1) / 2; const dx = objCx - char.tx; const dy = objCy - char.ty; if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) { char._updateFacing(dx, 0); } else { char._updateFacing(0, dy); } ``` So the facing logic already exists in `_doInteraction`. But the issue description mentions `_handleObjectArrival` and `_startConversation` which don't exist in the current code. It seems like this has already been partially fixed - the `_doInteraction` method already handles facing. Let me check if there's a `_start` method that might need updating.      1→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     2→// Character System — Movement, Perception, A* Pathfinding
     3→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     4→//
     5→// Characters have: id, name, personality, position, action state,
     6→// mood, energy, facing direction. They move between tiles using
     7→// A* pathfinding on the walkable tilemap.
     8→//
     9→// Walk animation alternates walk1/walk2 sprites while moving.
    10→// Perception system returns nearby objects and characters within radius.
    11→
    12→import { MAP, T, MAP_COLS, MAP_ROWS, TILE_SIZE } from './tilemap.js';
    13→
    14→// ── Walkable tiles (everything except walls, fences, water) ──
    15→const UNWALKABLE = new Set([T.WALL, T.WALL_TOP, T.COUNTER, T.COUNTER_L, T.COUNTER_R, T.WINDOW]);
    16→
    17→export function isWalkable(tx, ty) {
    18→  if (tx < 0 || tx >= MAP_COLS || ty < 0 || ty >= MAP_ROWS) return false;
    19→  return !UNWALKABLE.has(MAP[ty][tx]);
    20→}
    21→
    22→// ── A* Pathfinding ──
    23→// Returns array of {tx, ty} waypoints (excludes start, includes goal),
    24→// or null if no path found. Returns [] if already at goal.
    25→
    26→const NEIGHBORS = [[0, -1], [0, 1], [-1, 0], [1, 0]];
    27→
    28→export function findPath(sx, sy, gx, gy) {
    29→  if (!isWalkable(gx, gy)) return null;
    30→
    31→  const startKey = sy * MAP_COLS + sx;
    32→  const goalKey = gy * MAP_COLS + gx;
    33→  if (startKey === goalKey) return [];
    34→
    35→  const open = [startKey];
    36→  const cameFrom = new Map();
    37→  const gScore = new Map([[startKey, 0]]);
    38→  const fScore = new Map([[startKey, Math.abs(sx - gx) + Math.abs(sy - gy)]]);
    39→  const closed = new Set();
    40→
    41→  while (open.length > 0) {
    42→    // Find node with lowest fScore
    43→    let bestIdx = 0;
    44→    let bestF = fScore.get(open[0]) ?? Infinity;
    45→    for (let i = 1; i < open.length; i++) {
    46→      const f = fScore.get(open[i]) ?? Infinity;
    47→      if (f < bestF) { bestF = f; bestIdx = i; }
    48→    }
    49→
    50→    const current = open[bestIdx];
    51→    if (current === goalKey) {
    52→      const path = [];
    53→      let c = current;
    54→      while (cameFrom.has(c)) {
    55→        path.unshift({ tx: c % MAP_COLS, ty: Math.floor(c / MAP_COLS) });
    56→        c = cameFrom.get(c);
    57→      }
    58→      return path;
    59→    }
    60→
    61→    open.splice(bestIdx, 1);
    62→    closed.add(current);
    63→
    64→    const cx = current % MAP_COLS;
    65→    const cy = Math.floor(current / MAP_COLS);
    66→
    67→    for (const [dx, dy] of NEIGHBORS) {
    68→      const nx = cx + dx;
    69→      const ny = cy + dy;
    70→      if (!isWalkable(nx, ny)) continue;
    71→
    72→      const nKey = ny * MAP_COLS + nx;
    73→      if (closed.has(nKey)) continue;
    74→
    75→      const tentG = (gScore.get(current) ?? Infinity) + 1;
    76→      if (tentG < (gScore.get(nKey) ?? Infinity)) {
    77→        cameFrom.set(nKey, current);
    78→        gScore.set(nKey, tentG);
    79→        fScore.set(nKey, tentG + Math.abs(nx - gx) + Math.abs(ny - gy));
    80→        if (!open.includes(nKey)) open.push(nKey);
    81→      }
    82→    }
    83→  }
    84→
    85→  return null; // no path
    86→}
    87→
    88→// ── Find walkable tile adjacent to an object (for interaction) ──
    89→export function findInteractTile(objPosition) {
    90→  const { tx, ty, tw = 1, th = 1 } = objPosition;
    91→  const candidates = [];
    92→
    93→  for (let x = tx - 1; x <= tx + tw; x++) {
    94→    if (isWalkable(x, ty - 1)) candidates.push({ tx: x, ty: ty - 1 });
    95→    if (isWalkable(x, ty + th)) candidates.push({ tx: x, ty: ty + th });
    96→  }
    97→  for (let y = ty; y < ty + th; y++) {
    98→    if (isWalkable(tx - 1, y)) candidates.push({ tx: tx - 1, ty: y });
    99→    if (isWalkable(tx + tw, y)) candidates.push({ tx: tx + tw, ty: y });
   100→  }
   101→
   102→  if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
   103→  return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
   104→}

   106→// ── Character class ──
   107→
   108→export class Character {
   109→  constructor(def) {
   110→    this.id = def.id;
   111→    this.name = def.name;
   112→    this.personality = def.personality;
   113→    this.tx = def.tx;
   114→    this.ty = def.ty;

   120→
   121→    // Movement
   122→    this.path = [];          // waypoints to follow
   123→    this.moveProgress = 0;   // 0–1 progress toward next waypoint
   124→    this.moveSpeed = 2.0;    // tiles per second
   125→    this.prevTx = def.tx;
   126→    this.prevTy = def.ty;
   127→
   128→    // Walk animation (4-frame cycle: walk1→walk2→walk3→walk4)
   129→    this.walkFrame = 0;      // 0–3 → walk1/walk2/walk3/walk4
   130→    this.walkTimer = 0;
   131→    this.walkFrameMs = 200;  // ms between frame advances
   132→
   133→    // Wander AI
   134→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   135→    this.wanderCooldown = 2000 + Math.random() * 5000; // start soon
   136→    this.interactTimer = 0;
   137→
   138→    // Interaction tracking
   139→    this.lastObjectId = null;
   140→    this.pendingAction = 'use';
   141→
   142→    // Mood system
   143→    this.mood = 'content';       // happy | content | neutral | upset
   144→    this.moodTimer = 0;          // ms until mood resets to content
   145→  }
   146→
   147→  /** Sprite key for the current animation frame. */
   148→  get spriteKey() {
   149→    if (this.action === 'walking') {
   150→      return `${this.id}_walk${this.walkFrame + 1}`;
   151→    }
   152→    return `${this.id}_idle`;
   153→  }
   154→
   155→  get moodEmoji() {
   156→    switch (this.mood) {
   157→      case 'happy': return '😊';
   158→      case 'content': return '😌';
   159→      case 'upset': return '😤';
   160→      default: return null;
   161→    }
   162→  }
   163→
   164→  /** Pixel X position (interpolated between tiles for smooth movement). */
   165→  get px() {
   166→    if (this.path.length === 0) return this.tx * TILE_SIZE;
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  /** Pixel Y position (interpolated between tiles for smooth movement). */
   172→  get py() {
   173→    if (this.path.length === 0) return this.ty * TILE_SIZE;
   174→    const next = this.path[0];
   175→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE;
   176→  }
   177→
   178→  /** Start moving toward a goal tile. Returns true if a path was found. */
   179→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   180→    const path = findPath(Math.round(this.tx), Math.round(this.ty), goalTx, goalTy);
   181→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   182→      this.path = path;
   183→      this.prevTx = Math.round(this.tx);
   184→      this.prevTy = Math.round(this.ty);
   185→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   186→      this.action = 'walking';
   187→      this._updateFacing(path[0].tx - this.prevTx, path[0].ty - this.prevTy);
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Per-frame update: advance position and animation. */
   194→  update(deltaMs) {
   195→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   196→      // Walk animation cycle (4 frames)
   197→      this.walkTimer += deltaMs;
   198→      if (this.walkTimer >= this.walkFrameMs) {
   199→        this.walkTimer -= this.walkFrameMs;
   200→        this.walkFrame = (this.walkFrame + 1) % 4;
   201→      }
   202→
   203→      // Advance position along path
   204→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   205→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   206→
   207→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   208→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   209→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   210→        this.tx = arrived.tx;
   211→        this.ty = arrived.ty;
   212→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   213→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   214→
   215→        if (this.path.length > 0) {
   216→          this._updateFacing(this.path[0].tx - this.tx, this.path[0].ty - this.ty);
   217→        }
   218→      }
   219→
   220→      // Arrived at destination
   221→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   222→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   223→        this.action = 'idle';
   224→      }
   225→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   226→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   227→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   228→        this.action = 'idle';
   229→        this.targetObjectId = null;
   230→      }
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Decay mood back to content
   234→    if (this.moodTimer > 0) {
   235→      this.moodTimer -= deltaMs;
   236→      if (this.moodTimer <= 0) {
   237→        this.mood = 'content';
   238→        this.moodTimer = 0;
   239→      }
   240→    }
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  _updateFacing(dx, dy) {
   244→    if (dx > 0) this.facing = 'right';
   245→    else if (dx < 0) this.facing = 'left';
   246→    else if (dy > 0) this.facing = 'down';
   247→    else if (dy < 0) this.facing = 'up';
   248→  }
   249→
   250→  /** Enter interaction state (after arriving at an object). */
   251→  startInteraction(objectId) {
   252→    this.action = 'interacting';
   253→    this.targetObjectId = objectId;
   254→    this.lastObjectId = objectId;
   255→    this.interactTimer = 2000;
   256→  }
   257→
   258→  setMood(mood, durationMs = 15000) {
   259→    this.mood = mood;
   260→    this.moodTimer = durationMs;
   261→  }
   262→
   263→  /** Get nearby objects and characters within Manhattan distance radius. */
   264→  getPerception(objects, characters, radius = 5) {
   265→    const nearbyObjects = [];
   266→    const nearbyCharacters = [];
   267→
   268→    for (const obj of objects) {
   269→      const dist = Math.abs(obj.position.tx - this.tx) + Math.abs(obj.position.ty - this.ty);
   270→      if (dist <= radius) {
   271→        nearbyObjects.push({
   272→          id: obj.id,
   273→          name: obj.name,
   274→          state: obj.state,
   275→          distance: dist,
   276→          sector: obj.sector,
   277→        });
   278→      }
   279→    }
   280→
   281→    for (const char of characters) {
   282→      if (char.id === this.id) continue;
   283→      const dist = Math.abs(char.tx - this.tx) + Math.abs(char.ty - this.ty);
   284→      if (dist <= radius) {
   285→        nearbyCharacters.push({
   286→          id: char.id,
   287→          name: char.name,
   288→          action: char.action,
   289→          distance: dist,
   290→        });
   291→      }
   292→    }
   293→
   294→    return { objects: nearbyObjects, characters: nearbyCharacters };
   295→  }
   296→}

    10→import { findInteractTile } from './characters.js';
    11→import { SECTORS } from './world.js';
    12→
    13→const STAGGER_MS = 12000;
    14→const COOLDOWN_MIN = 30000;
    15→const COOLDOWN_MAX = 60000;
    16→
    17→export class AIDecisionEngine {
    18→  constructor(options = {}) {
    19→    this.client = new AIClient({
    20→      endpoint: options.endpoint || '',
    21→      timeoutMs: options.timeoutMs || 15000,
    22→    });
    23→    this.engine = null;
    24→    this.charState = new Map();
    25→    this.pendingMessages = new Map(); // charId → [{ from, dialogue }]
    26→  }
    27→
    28→  /** Link to the simulation engine (called once during setup). */
    29→  attach(engine) {
    30→    this.engine = engine;
    31→    this.charState.clear();
    32→    this.pendingMessages.clear();
    33→    engine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
    34→      this.charState.set(char.id, {
    35→        cooldownMs: 5000 + i * STAGGER_MS,
    36→        pending: false,
    37→      });
    38→    });
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  setEndpoint(url) {
    42→    this.client.endpoint = url;
    43→  }
    44→
    45→  get endpoint() {
    46→    return this.client.endpoint;
    47→  }
    48→
    49→  /** Returns true if this character has a pending AI decision. */
    50→  isPending(charId) {
    51→    return this.charState.get(charId)?.pending || false;
    52→  }
    53→
    54→  /** Called each engine tick for each idle character. */
    55→  tick(char, deltaMs) {
    56→    const state = this.charState.get(char.id);
    57→    if (!state || state.pending) return;
    58→
    59→    state.cooldownMs -= deltaMs;
    60→    if (state.cooldownMs > 0) return;
    61→
    62→    state.cooldownMs = COOLDOWN_MIN + Math.random() * (COOLDOWN_MAX - COOLDOWN_MIN);
    63→    state.pending = true;
    64→
    65→    this._requestDecision(char).catch(() => {});
    66→  }
    67→
    68→  async _requestDecision(char) {
    69→    const state = this.charState.get(char.id);
    70→    const engineRef = this.engine;
    71→
    72→    try {
    73→      if (!this.client.endpoint) {
    74→        throw new Error('No API endpoint configured');
    75→      }
    76→
    77→      const objects = engineRef.objectEngine.getAll();
    78→      const characters = engineRef.characters;
    79→      const perception = char.getPerception(objects, characters);
    80→
    81→      // Attach pending messages from other characters
    82→      const messages = this.pendingMessages.get(char.id);
    83→      if (messages && messages.length > 0) {
    84→        perception.recentMessages = messages.slice();
    85→        this.pendingMessages.delete(char.id);
    86→      }
    87→
    88→      const decision = await this.client.decide({
    89→        character: char.name,
    90→        personality: char.personality,
    91→        perception,
    92→        mood: char.mood,
    93→        energy: char.energy,
    94→        time: engineRef.simClock.timeString,
    95→        day: engineRef.simClock.day,
    96→      });
    97→
    98→      // Engine might have been reset while we waited
    99→      if (this.engine !== engineRef) return;
   100→      if (char.action !== 'idle') return;
   101→
   102→      this._executeDecision(char, decision);
   103→    } catch (err) {
   104→      if (this.engine !== engineRef) return;
   105→      console.warn(`AI decision failed for ${char.name}:`, err.message || err);
   106→      if (char.action === 'idle') {
   107→        engineRef._randomWander(char);
   108→      }
   109→    } finally {
   110→      state.pending = false;
   111→    }
   112→  }
   113→
   114→  _executeDecision(char, decision) {
   115→    if (!decision || !decision.action) return;
   116→
   117→    const engine = this.engine;
   118→    const objects = engine.objectEngine.getAll();
   119→    const characters = engine.characters;
   120→
   121→    // Emit description for status bar
   122→    if (decision.description) {
   123→      engine._emit('ai:status', {
   124→        characterName: char.name,
   125→        description: decision.description,
   126→      });
   127→    }
   128→
   129→    switch (decision.action) {
   130→      case 'interact': {
   131→        const obj = this._resolveObject(decision.target, objects);
   132→        if (!obj) {
   133→          engine._randomWander(char);
   134→          return;
   135→        }
   136→
   137→        const tile = findInteractTile(obj.position);
   138→        if (!tile) {
   139→          engine._randomWander(char);
   140→          return;
   141→        }
   142→
   143→        const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);
   144→        if (atTarget) {
   145→          engine._doInteraction(char, obj, 'use');
   146→        } else if (char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   147→          char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   148→          char.pendingAction = 'use';
   149→        }
   150→
   151→        if (decision.dialogue) {
   152→          engine._emit('ai:speech', { characterId: char.id, dialogue: decision.dialogue });
   153→        }
   154→        break;
   155→      }
   156→
   157→      case 'move': {
   158→        const sector = this._resolveSector(decision.target);
   159→        if (sector) {
   160→          const ox = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) - 1;
   161→          const oy = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) - 1;
   162→          char.moveTo(sector.tx + ox, sector.ty + oy);
   163→        }
   164→
   165→        if (decision.dialogue) {
   166→          engine._emit('ai:speech', { characterId: char.id, dialogue: decision.dialogue });
   167→        }
   168→        break;
   169→      }
   170→
   171→      case 'talk': {
   172→        const target = characters.find(c =>
   173→          c.id !== char.id && (
   174→            c.name.toLowerCase() === (decision.target || '').toLowerCase() ||
   175→            c.id === (decision.target || '').toLowerCase()
   176→          )
   177→        );
   178→
   179→        if (decision.dialogue) {
   180→          engine._emit('ai:speech', { characterId: char.id, dialogue: decision.dialogue });
   181→        }
   182→
   183→        if (target) {
   184→          // Queue message for target's next decision
   185→          if (!this.pendingMessages.has(target.id)) {
   186→            this.pendingMessages.set(target.id, []);
   187→          }
   188→          this.pendingMessages.get(target.id).push({
   189→            from: char.name,
   190→            dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   191→          });
   192→
   193→          // Move toward the target if far away
   194→          const dist = Math.abs(char.tx - target.tx) + Math.abs(char.ty - target.ty);
   195→          if (dist > 2) {
   196→            const adjTile = findInteractTile({
   197→              tx: Math.round(target.tx), ty: Math.round(target.ty), tw: 1, th: 1,
   198→            });
   199→            if (adjTile) char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty);
   200→          }
   201→
   202→          // Bump target's cooldown so they respond sooner
   203→          const targetState = this.charState.get(target.id);
   204→          if (targetState && !targetState.pending) {
   205→            targetState.cooldownMs = Math.min(targetState.cooldownMs, 8000 + Math.random() * 4000);
   206→          }
   207→        }
   208→        break;
   209→      }
   210→
   211→      case 'idle': {
   212→        // Character stays put — just show dialogue
   213→        if (decision.dialogue) {
   214→          engine._emit('ai:speech', { characterId: char.id, dialogue: decision.dialogue });
   215→        }
   216→        break;
   217→      }
   218→
   219→      default:
   220→        engine._randomWander(char);
   221→    }
   222→  }
   223→
   224→  _resolveObject(target, objects) {
   225→    if (!target) return null;
   226→    const lower = target.toLowerCase();
   227→    const underscored = lower.replace(/\s+/g, '_');
   228→    return objects.find(o => o.id === target) ||
   229→      objects.find(o => o.id === underscored) ||
   230→      objects.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === lower) ||
   231→      objects.find(o => o.id.endsWith(underscored)) ||
   232→      objects.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase().includes(lower)) ||
   233→      null;
   234→  }
   235→
   236→  _resolveSector(target) {
   237→    if (!target) return null;
   238→    const lower = target.toLowerCase();
   239→    if (SECTORS[lower]) return SECTORS[lower];
   240→    return Object.values(SECTORS).find(s =>
   241→      s.name.toLowerCase() === lower
   242→    ) || null;
   243→  }
   244→}
   245→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #34
Now I understand the codebase. Let me analyze what's missing and what needs to be implemented: 1. **Object facing in `_doInteraction`** - Already implemented! Lines 301-310 of engine.js already calculate the facing direction from character to object and set it. So this part is done. 2. **Character conversation facing** - In `ai.js`, the `talk` action (lines 171-208) moves a character toward the target character, but when they arrive, there's no facing logic. The character moves to an adjacent tile but never faces the target character. Looking at the `talk` case: The code moves the character toward the target if they're more than 2 tiles away, but once they're close enough (dist <= 2), nothing happens to make them face each other. I need to add facing logic that calculates the direction between the two characters and sets their facing when they're adjacent. I see the issue now—when characters move toward each other for conversations, the `targetObjectId` stays null since they're targeting another character, not an object, so the facing logic in `_doInteraction` never triggers. The issue description mentions methods like `_handleObjectArrival` and `_startConversation` that don't exist in the current codebase, which means I need to figure out where the facing logic should actually be implemented. Looking at the existing facing code in `_doInteraction`, it calculates the direction from the character to the object's center and updates facing accordingly—this part seems to already be working for objects. But for character-to-character interactions, there's no equivalent facing setup happening when they arrive at their destination. there. So either the issue was created before this code was added, or there's still a conversation-facing problem. Looking at the git history, the most recent commit doesn't seem related to the facing fix, so let me dig deeper into how `_doInteraction` and the `talk` action actually work. I see that `_doInteraction` handles facing, but when characters talk to each other in `ai.js`, there's a gap: if they're close enough (dist <= 2), they talk without moving and never face the target. If they move closer (dist > 2), they arrive at an adjacent tile but `targetObjectId` is never set for character-to-character conversations, so `_doInteraction` never gets called to update facing. The acceptance criteria clearly states characters should face each other during conversations, and that's not happening. I need to fix this by either adding a `targetCharId` field to track character-to-character interactions separately, or handling the facing update differently in the `talk` action logic itself. When the character is already close enough, I can call `_updateFacing` directly with the direction toward the target. If they need to move first, I should set a `pendingFaceCharId` property that triggers facing behavior once they arrive at their destination, similar to how `pendingAction` works in the existing character update logic. I need to make sure character-to-character interactions have the facing logic too — when two characters talk, they should face each other, and this should happen immediately when the conversation starts, not just when they arrive. Let me verify what's already working: objects get the facing update in `_doInteraction`, but for characters I'm missing that piece. The real gap is making sure both participants in a conversation orient toward each other. Does the object facing code in `_doInteraction` already cover the case where a character is "already adjacent" (atTarget case in `_wanderTick`)? Let me trace through this: when a character reaches their target tile in `_wanderTick`, it calls `_doInteraction` which handles the facing direction. And in `_updateCharacters`, when a character finishes walking to an object, `_doInteraction` gets called again to set the facing. So object facing is fully covered. For conversation facing in `ai.js`, the `talk` case handles it in two scenarios: if the target is already close (within 2 tiles), the character faces them immediately, otherwise they face toward the target once they arrive. Now I need to check whether the `talk` case sets `char.targetObjectId` and trace through the pathfinding logic... Checking the talk case implementation... Setting up character-to-character facing by adding a `targetCharId` field and updating the `talk` case to handle mutual facing when characters are close or when they arrive at their destination. Setting up mutual facing logic... I need to make sure `targetCharId` gets cleared when a character starts moving toward an object, so it doesn't conflict with `targetObjectId`. Looking at the flow, when `moveTo` is called for an object target, I should clear any existing `targetCharId` to prevent the facing logic from triggering incorrectly when the character arrives. Alternatively, I could handle both arrival scenarios in `_updateCharacters` and unconditionally clear `targetCharId` after processing, whether it's an object interaction or a character interaction.    105→test('ObjectInstance: initial state', () => {
   106→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   107→  assert(obj.state === 'off', 'oven starts in off state');
   108→  assert(obj.visual === 'oven_off', 'visual matches off state');
   109→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === null, 'no auto_next timer when off');
   110→});
   111→
   112→test('ObjectInstance: character interaction triggers transition', () => {
   113→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   114→  const event = obj.interact('use');
   115→  assert(event !== null, 'interact returns an event');
   116→  assert(event.from === 'off', 'event.from is off');
   117→  assert(event.to === 'preheating', 'event.to is preheating');
   118→  assert(obj.state === 'preheating', 'oven is now preheating');
   119→  assert(obj.visual === 'oven_glow', 'visual is oven_glow');
   120→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 30000, 'auto_next timer is 30s');
   121→});
   122→
   123→test('ObjectInstance: invalid interaction returns null', () => {
   124→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   125→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   126→  const event = obj.interact('use'); // preheating has no 'use' transition
   127→  assert(event === null, 'no valid transition returns null');
   128→});
   129→
   130→test('ObjectInstance: auto_next timer fires', () => {
   131→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   132→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   133→
   134→  // Tick for less than 30s — no transition
   135→  let event = obj.tick(15000);
   136→  assert(event === null, 'no transition before timer expires');
   137→  assert(obj.state === 'preheating', 'still preheating');
   138→  assert(obj.timer === 15000, 'timer advanced');
   139→
   140→  // Tick past the 30s mark
   141→  event = obj.tick(16000); // total: 31s
   142→  assert(event !== null, 'transition fires after timer expires');
   143→  assert(event.from === 'preheating', 'from preheating');
   144→  assert(event.to === 'baking', 'to baking');
   145→  assert(event.trigger === 'auto', 'trigger is auto');
   146→  assert(obj.state === 'baking', 'oven is now baking');
   147→});
   148→
   149→test('ObjectInstance: full auto-transition chain (preheating → baking → done → burnt)', () => {
   150→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   151→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   152→
   153→  // preheating → baking (30s)
   154→  obj.tick(30000);
   155→  assert(obj.state === 'baking', 'preheating → baking after 30s');
   156→
   157→  // baking → done (60s)
   158→  obj.tick(60000);
   159→  assert(obj.state === 'done', 'baking → done after 60s');
   160→
   161→  // done → burnt (30s)
   162→  obj.tick(30000);
   163→  assert(obj.state === 'burnt', 'done → burnt after 30s');
   164→
   165→  // burnt has no auto_next — stays burnt
   166→  obj.tick(60000);
   167→  assert(obj.state === 'burnt', 'burnt stays burnt (no auto_next)');
   168→});
   169→
   170→test('ObjectInstance: interaction at done state prevents burning', () => {
   171→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   172→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating
   173→  obj.tick(30000);     // → baking
   174→  obj.tick(60000);     // → done
   175→
   176→  // Character takes the bread before it burns
   177→  const event = obj.interact('use');
   178→  assert(event !== null, 'interaction at done succeeds');
   179→  assert(event.to === 'off', 'oven returns to off');
   180→  assert(event.produces === 'bread', 'produces bread');
   181→  assert(event.target === 'bakery_display_case', 'target is display case');
   182→  assert(obj.state === 'off', 'oven is off');
   183→});
   184→
   185→test('ObjectEngine: tick advances all objects', () => {
   186→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   187→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   188→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   189→
   190→  // Start the oven
   191→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   192→
   193→  // Tick — only oven has a timer
   194→  let events = engine.tick(30000);
   195→  assert(events.length === 1, 'one transition event');
   196→  assert(events[0].objectId === 'bakery_oven', 'event is from oven');
   197→  assert(events[0].to === 'baking', 'oven transitioned to baking');
   198→});
   199→
   200→test('ObjectEngine: production side-effect (oven → display case)', () => {
   201→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   202→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   203→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   204→
   205→  // Run oven through to done
   206→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   207→  engine.tick(30000);                     // → baking
   208→  engine.tick(60000);                     // → done
   209→
   210→  // Character takes bread out
   211→  const event = engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use');
   212→  assert(event.produces === 'bread', 'oven produces bread');
   213→
   214→  // Check display case got the bread
   215→  const display = engine.get('bakery_display_case');
   216→  assert(display.state === 'bread', 'display case now has bread');
   217→});
   218→
   219→test('ObjectEngine: event listeners fire', () => {
   220→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   221→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   222→
   223→  const received = [];
   224→  engine.onTransition((event) => received.push(event));
   225→
   226→  engine.interact('bakery_oven', 'use'); // → preheating
   227→  assert(received.length === 1, 'listener received interaction event');
   228→  assert(received[0].to === 'preheating', 'event has correct target state');
   229→
   230→  engine.tick(30000); // → baking
   231→  assert(received.length === 2, 'listener received auto-transition event');
   232→});
   233→
   234→test('ObjectEngine: getBySector filters correctly', () => {
   235→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   236→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   237→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   238→  engine.addObject({
   239→    id: 'studio_easel',
   240→    name: 'easel',
   241→    sector: 'studio',
   242→    arena: 'workspace',
   243→    position: { x: 400, y: 430 },
   244→    state: 'blank',
   245→    states: { blank: { visual: 'easel_blank' } },
   246→  });
   247→
   248→  const bakeryObjects = engine.getBySector('bakery');
   249→  assert(bakeryObjects.length === 2, 'bakery has 2 objects');
   250→
   251→  const studioObjects = engine.getBySector('studio');
   252→  assert(studioObjects.length === 1, 'studio has 1 object');
   253→});
   254→
   255→test('ObjectEngine: snapshot returns all object states', () => {
   256→  const engine = new ObjectEngine();
   257→  engine.addObject(makeOvenDef());
   258→  engine.addObject(makeDisplayCaseDef());
   259→
   260→  const snap = engine.snapshot();
   261→  assert('bakery_oven' in snap, 'snapshot has oven');
   262→  assert('bakery_display_case' in snap, 'snapshot has display case');
   263→  assert(snap.bakery_oven.state === 'off', 'oven state is off');
   264→  assert(snap.bakery_display_case.state === 'empty', 'display case is empty');
   265→});
   266→
   267→test('ObjectInstance: timeRemainingMs tracks correctly', () => {
   268→  const obj = new ObjectInstance(makeOvenDef());
   269→  obj.interact('use'); // → preheating, 30s timer
   270→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 30000, 'full 30s remaining');
   271→
   272→  obj.tick(10000);
   273→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 20000, '20s remaining after 10s tick');
   274→
   275→  obj.tick(10000);
   276→  assert(obj.timeRemainingMs === 10000, '10s remaining after 20s total');
   277→});
   278→
   279→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   280→// Report
   281→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   282→
   283→console.log(`
${'═'.repeat(50)}`);
   284→console.log(`Object State Machine Tests`);
   285→console.log(`${'═'.repeat(50)}`);
   286→

   288→  console.log(`  ${r.ok ? '✓' : '✗'} ${r.name}${r.error ? ` (${r.error})` : ''}`);
   289→}
   290→

  ${passed} passed, ${failed} failed, ${passed + failed} total`);
   292→console.log(`${'═'.repeat(50)}

{"id":"ca92ff28-607b-4f65-aad6-a4666801e942","identifier":"FRG-244","title":"Characters face toward objects when interacting","description":"## Problem

When a character arrives at an object, they keep whatever facing direction they had from walking. Sol uses the kotatsu but faces left instead of toward it.

## Root Cause

\\_handleObjectArrival in Engine.js calls char.startInteraction() but never sets char.facing based on the object position.

## What to do

1. In \\_handleObjectArrival, calculate facing direction from character position to object tile
2. Set char.facing before calling startInteraction()
3. Same for \\_startConversation — characters should face each other

## Acceptance Criteria

* Character faces the object they are interacting with
* Characters face each other during conversations

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #82
## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`src/characters.js`**: Added `targetCharId = null` field to Character constructor — tracks which character to face toward upon arrival - **`src/engine.js`**: Refactored `_updateCharacters` arrival check to handle both `targetObjectId` (object interaction, already had facing via `_doInteraction`) and new `targetCharId` (conversation — faces both characters toward each other on arrival) - **`src/ai.js`**: Updated `talk` case to face both characters toward each other immediately when already close (dist ≤ 2), or set `char.targetCharId` when moving toward the talk target so facing is applied on arrival ## Key Decisions - Object-facing was already implemented in `_doInteraction` (the issue description referenced method names from an older version of the code) — no changes needed there - The conversation facing applies to both the initiating character and the target, covering the "face each other" acceptance criterion - `targetCharId` is cleared after use to avoid stale state; it takes effect only when `targetObjectId` is null, so object interactions naturally take priority ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-244-characters-face-toward-objects-when-interacting` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium/pull/3
